<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h3 id="3.3.-Common-Table-Expressions">3.3. Common Table Expressions<a class="anchor-link" href="#3.3.-Common-Table-Expressions">&#182;</a></h3><p><strong> Common Table Expressions (CTEs) </strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Query complexity increases quickly!<ul>
<li>Information can be difficult to keep track of</li>
<li>SOLUTION: CTEs</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>How to use CTEs?<ul>
<li>Table declared before the main query.<ul>
<li><code>WITH</code> cte_name <code>AS</code>(subquery)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Named and referenced later in FROM statement.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Why use CTEs?<ul>
<li>Executed only once, then stored in memory<ul>
<li>Improves query performance</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Improving organization of queries</li>
<li>Referencing other CTEs</li>
<li>Referencing itself (SELF JOIN)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="3.3.1.-Example:-CTEs-with-Nested-Subqueries">3.3.1. Example: CTEs with Nested Subqueries<a class="anchor-link" href="#3.3.1.-Example:-CTEs-with-Nested-Subqueries">&#182;</a></h4><p>Declare a CTE that calculates the total goals from matches in August of the 2013/2014 season. And according to the CTE, calculate the average goals of each country in August during that season.</p>

</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[72]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;-- Set up your CTE</span>
<span class="s2">WITH match_list AS (</span>
<span class="s2">    SELECT </span>
<span class="s2">        country_id,</span>
<span class="s2">       (home_team_goal + away_team_goal) AS goals</span>
<span class="s2">    FROM match</span>
<span class="s2">    -- Create a list of match IDs to filter data in the CTE</span>
<span class="s2">    WHERE id IN (</span>
<span class="s2">       SELECT id</span>
<span class="s2">       FROM match</span>
<span class="s2">                                   -- EXTRACT(MONTH FROM date) = 08 -- Postgres Syntax</span>
<span class="s2">       WHERE season = &#39;2013/2014&#39; AND STRFTIME(&#39;%m&#39;, date) = &#39;08&#39;))</span>
<span class="s2">       </span>
<span class="s2">-- Select the league name and average of goals in the CTE</span>
<span class="s2">SELECT </span>
<span class="s2">    l.name,</span>
<span class="s2">    AVG(goals)</span>
<span class="s2">FROM league AS l</span>
<span class="s2">-- Join the CTE onto the league table</span>
<span class="s2">LEFT JOIN match_list ON l.id = match_list.country_id</span>
<span class="s2">GROUP BY l.name;</span>
<span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
<span class="n">pd</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">read_sql</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">conn</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="output_wrapper">
<div class="output">


<div class="output_area">

    <div class="prompt output_prompt">Out[72]:</div>



<div class="output_html rendered_html output_subarea output_execute_result">
<div>
<style scoped>
    .dataframe tbody tr th:only-of-type {
        vertical-align: middle;
    }

    .dataframe tbody tr th {
        vertical-align: top;
    }

    .dataframe thead th {
        text-align: right;
    }
</style>
<table border="1" class="dataframe">
  <thead>
    <tr style="text-align: right;">
      <th></th>
      <th>name</th>
      <th>AVG(goals)</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <th>0</th>
      <td>Belgium Jupiler League</td>
      <td>NaN</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <th>1</th>
      <td>England Premier League</td>
      <td>2.000000</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <th>2</th>
      <td>France Ligue 1</td>
      <td>2.027027</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <th>3</th>

      <td>3.235294</td>
    </tr>

      <th>4</th>
      <td>Italy Serie A</td>
      <td>2.750000</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>
</div>
</div>

</div>

</div>
</div>

</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing text_cell rendered"><div class="prompt input_prompt">
</div><div class="inner_cell">
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h3 id="3.4.-Wrap-Up:-Which-to-Use?">3.4. Wrap-Up: Which to Use?<a class="anchor-link" href="#3.4.-Wrap-Up:-Which-to-Use?">&#182;</a></h3><p><strong> Differentiating What You’ve Learned </strong></p>
<table>
<thead><tr>
<th style="text-align:center">Joins</th>
<th style="text-align:center">Correlated Subqueries</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center">Combine 2+ tables</td>
<td style="text-align:center">Match subqueries &amp; tables</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center">Simple</td>
<td style="text-align:center">Avoid limits of joins.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center">Operations / Aggregations</td>
<td style="text-align:center">High processing time</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center">Eg: What is the total sales per employee?</td>
<td style="text-align:center">Eg: Who does each employee report to in a company?</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table>
<thead><tr>
<th style="text-align:center">Multiple/Nested Subqueries</th>
<th style="text-align:center">Common Table Expressions</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center">Multi-step transformations</td>
<td style="text-align:center">Organize subqueries sequentially</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center">Improve accuracy and reproducibility</td>
<td style="text-align:center">Can reference other CTEs</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center">Eg: What is the average deal size closed by each sales representative in the quarter?</td>
<td style="text-align:center">Eg: How did the marketing,sales, growth, &amp; engineering teams perform on key metrics?</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong> Q: How do you get both the home and away team names into one final query result? </strong></p>
<h4 id="3.4.1.-Example:-With-a-Subquery">3.4.1. Example: With a Subquery<a class="anchor-link" href="#3.4.1.-Example:-With-a-Subquery">&#182;</a></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[73]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;SELECT</span>
<span class="s2">    m.date,</span>
<span class="s2">    -- Get the home and away team names</span>
<span class="s2">    hometeam,</span>
<span class="s2">    awayteam,</span>
<span class="s2">    m.home_team_goal,</span>
<span class="s2">    m.away_team_goal</span>
<span class="s2">FROM match AS m</span>
<span class="s2">-- Join the home subquery to the match table</span>
<span class="s2">LEFT JOIN (</span>
<span class="s2">  SELECT match.id, team.team_long_name AS hometeam</span>
<span class="s2">  FROM match</span>
<span class="s2">  LEFT JOIN team</span>
<span class="s2">  ON match.home_team_api_id = team.team_api_id) AS home</span>
<span class="s2">ON home.id = m.id</span>
<span class="s2">-- Join the away subquery to the match table</span>
<span class="s2">LEFT JOIN (</span>
<span class="s2">  SELECT match.id, team.team_long_name AS awayteam</span>
<span class="s2">  FROM match</span>
<span class="s2">  LEFT JOIN team</span>
<span class="s2">  -- Get the away team ID in the subquery</span>
<span class="s2">  ON match.away_team_api_id = team.team_api_id) AS away</span>
<span class="s2">ON away.id = m.id;</span>
<span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
<span class="n">pd</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">read_sql</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">conn</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="output">

<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h4 id="3.4.2.-Example:-With-Correlated-Subqueries">3.4.2. Example: With Correlated Subqueries<a class="anchor-link" href="#3.4.2.-Example:-With-Correlated-Subqueries">&#182;</a></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[74]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;SELECT</span>
<span class="s2">    m.date,</span>
<span class="s2">    (SELECT team_long_name</span>
<span class="s2">     FROM team AS t</span>
<span class="s2">     WHERE t.team_api_id = m.home_team_api_id) AS hometeam,</span>
<span class="s2">    -- Connect the team to the match table</span>
<span class="s2">    (SELECT team_long_name</span>
<span class="s2">     FROM team AS t</span>
<span class="s2">     WHERE t.team_api_id = m.away_team_api_id) AS awayteam,</span>
<span class="s2">    -- Select home and away goals</span>
<span class="s2">     home_team_goal,</span>
<span class="s2">     away_team_goal</span>
<span class="s2">FROM match AS m;</span>
<span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
<span class="n">pd</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">read_sql</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">conn</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>

<div class="cell border-box-sizing text_cell rendered"><div class="prompt input_prompt">
</div><div class="inner_cell">
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h4 id="3.4.3.-Example:-With-CTEs">3.4.3. Example: With CTEs<a class="anchor-link" href="#3.4.3.-Example:-With-CTEs">&#182;</a></h4>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[75]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;WITH home AS (</span>
<span class="s2">  SELECT m.id, m.date, </span>
<span class="s2">         t.team_long_name AS hometeam, m.home_team_goal</span>
<span class="s2">  FROM match AS m</span>
<span class="s2">  LEFT JOIN team AS t </span>
<span class="s2">  ON m.home_team_api_id = t.team_api_id),</span>
<span class="s2">-- Declare and set up the away CTE</span>
<span class="s2">away AS (</span>
<span class="s2">  SELECT m.id, m.date, </span>
<span class="s2">         t.team_long_name AS awayteam, m.away_team_goal</span>
<span class="s2">  FROM match AS m</span>
<span class="s2">  LEFT JOIN team AS t </span>
<span class="s2">  ON m.away_team_api_id = t.team_api_id)</span>
<span class="s2">-- Select date, home_goal, and away_goal</span>
<span class="s2">SELECT </span>
<span class="s2">    home.date,</span>
<span class="s2">    home.hometeam,</span>
<span class="s2">    away.awayteam,</span>
<span class="s2">    home.home_team_goal,</span>
<span class="s2">    away.away_team_goal</span>
<span class="s2">-- Join away and home on the id column</span>
<span class="s2">FROM home</span>
<span class="s2">INNER JOIN away</span>
<span class="s2">ON home.id = away.id;</span>
<span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
<span class="n">pd</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">read_sql</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">conn</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="output_wrapper">
<div class="output">


<div class="output_area">

    <div class="prompt output_prompt">Out[75]:</div>

<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<p>You now know three separate ways to manipulate and transform data to produce a complex query result! This is a great set of skills to have when working with complex relational databases!</p>

</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing text_cell rendered"><div class="prompt input_prompt">
</div><div class="inner_cell">
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h2 id="4.-Window-Functions">4. Window Functions<a class="anchor-link" href="#4.-Window-Functions">&#182;</a></h2><p>Learn about window functions and how to pass aggregate functions along a dataset. You will also learn how to calculate running totals and partitioned averages.</p>
<h3 id="4.1.-Window-Functions">4.1. Window Functions<a class="anchor-link" href="#4.1.-Window-Functions">&#182;</a></h3><p><strong> Why Need Window Functions?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>When working with AGGREGATE values, may want to use <code>GROUP BY</code><ul>
<li>Requires you to use <code>GROUP BY</code> with all non-aggregate columns, otherwise, raise ERROR.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[77]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">####### GIVES ERROR #######</span>
<span class="c1"># sql_stmt = &quot;&quot;&quot;SELECT</span>
<span class="c1">#   country_id,</span>
<span class="c1">#   season,</span>
<span class="c1">#   date,</span>
<span class="c1">#   AVG(home_goal) AS avg_home</span>
<span class="c1"># FROM match</span>
<span class="c1"># GROUP BY country_id;</span>
<span class="c1"># &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
<span class="c1"># pd.read_sql(sql_stmt, conn).head()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>
</div>
</div>

</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing text_cell rendered"><div class="prompt input_prompt">
</div><div class="inner_cell">
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<ul>
<li>Solution: Introducing window functions!<ul>
<li>Aggregate calculations</li>
<li>Similar to subqueries in SELECT</li>
<li>Running totals, rankings, moving averages</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Key differences<ul>
<li>Processed after every part of query except ORDER BY<ul>
<li>Uses information in result set rather than database</li>
<li>That is, unlike subquery, window functions apply your <code>WHERE</code> statement</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Available in PostgreSQL, Oracle, MySQL, SQL Server…<ul>
<li>…but NOT SQLite (Now available after v3.25)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Basic Syntax: Window_Func(.) OVER(...)</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="4.1.1.-Example:-Ranking-with-RANK()-&amp;-ORDER-BY">4.1.1. Example: Ranking with <code>RANK()</code> &amp; <code>ORDER BY</code><a class="anchor-link" href="#4.1.1.-Example:-Ranking-with-RANK()-&amp;-ORDER-BY">&#182;</a></h4><p>Create a data set of ranked matches according to which leagues, on average, score the most goals in a match.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>RANK()</code>: The window funciton using here<ul>
<li>Create a RANK of information according to any variable to sort your data.</li>
<li>Need to specify what column/calculation you want to use to calculate your rank.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>ORDER BY</code>: The sub-clause using here<ul>
<li>Execute the window function based on the order specified here.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[78]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;SELECT </span>
<span class="s2">    -- Select the league name and average goals scored</span>
<span class="s2">    l.name AS league,</span>
<span class="s2">    AVG(m.home_team_goal + m.away_team_goal) AS avg_goals,</span>
<span class="s2">    -- Rank each league according to the average goals</span>
<span class="s2">    RANK() OVER(ORDER BY AVG(m.home_team_goal + m.away_team_goal) DESC) AS league_rank</span>
<span class="s2">FROM league AS l</span>
<span class="s2">LEFT JOIN match AS m </span>
<span class="s2">ON l.id = m.country_id</span>
<span class="s2">WHERE m.season = &#39;2011/2012&#39;</span>
<span class="s2">GROUP BY l.name</span>
<span class="s2">-- Order the query by the rank you created</span>
<span class="s2">ORDER BY league_rank;</span>
<span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
<span class="n">pd</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">read_sql</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">conn</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="output_wrapper">
<div class="output">


<div class="output_area">

    <div class="prompt output_prompt">Out[78]:</div>

    }

<div class="cell border-box-sizing text_cell rendered"><div class="prompt input_prompt">
</div><div class="inner_cell">
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<p>Unlike a subquery in SELECT, your window function will apply the filter that you include in your WHERE clause.</p>
<h3 id="4.2.-Window-Partition">4.2. Window Partition<a class="anchor-link" href="#4.2.-Window-Partition">&#182;</a></h3><p><strong> <code>OVER</code> and <code>PARTITION BY</code></strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Calculate separate values for different categories</li>
<li>Calculate different calculations in the same column</li>
<li>Can partition data by 1 or more columns</li>
<li>Can partition aggregate calculations, ranks, etc</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="4.2.1.-Example:-PARTITION-BY-Multiple-Columns">4.2.1. Example: <code>PARTITION BY</code> Multiple Columns<a class="anchor-link" href="#4.2.1.-Example:-PARTITION-BY-Multiple-Columns">&#182;</a></h4><p>Calculate the average number home and away goals scored Legia Warszawa, and their opponents, partitioned by the month in each season.</p>

</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[79]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;SELECT </span>
<span class="s2">    date,</span>
<span class="s2">    season,</span>
<span class="s2">    home_team_goal,</span>
<span class="s2">    away_team_goal,</span>
<span class="s2">    CASE WHEN home_team_api_id = 8673 THEN &#39;home&#39; </span>
<span class="s2">         ELSE &#39;away&#39; END AS warsaw_location,</span>
<span class="s2">    -- Calculate average goals partitioned by season and month</span>
<span class="s2">    AVG(home_team_goal) OVER(PARTITION BY season, </span>
<span class="s2">          -- EXTRACT(MONTH FROM date) -- Postgres Syntax</span>
<span class="s2">            STRFTIME(&#39;%m&#39;, date)) AS season_mo_home,</span>
<span class="s2">    AVG(away_team_goal) OVER(PARTITION BY season,</span>
<span class="s2">          -- EXTRACT(MONTH FROM date) -- Postgres Syntax</span>
<span class="s2">          STRFTIME(&#39;%m&#39;, date)) AS season_mo_away</span>
<span class="s2">FROM match</span>
<span class="s2">WHERE </span>
<span class="s2">    home_team_api_id = 8673 </span>
<span class="s2">    OR away_team_api_id = 8673</span>
<span class="s2">ORDER BY (home_team_goal + away_team_goal) DESC;</span>
<span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
<span class="n">pd</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">read_sql</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">conn</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="output_wrapper">
<div class="output">


<div class="output_area">

    <div class="prompt output_prompt">Out[79]:</div>

<div class="cell border-box-sizing text_cell rendered"><div class="prompt input_prompt">
</div><div class="inner_cell">
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h3 id="4.3.-Sliding-Windows">4.3. Sliding Windows<a class="anchor-link" href="#4.3.-Sliding-Windows">&#182;</a></h3><p><strong> Sliding Windows </strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Perform calculations relative to the current row (default)<ul>
<li><code>n PRECEDING</code>: Select from <code>n</code> row before the current one</li>
<li><code>FOLLOWING</code>: Select until <code>n</code> row after the current one</li>
<li><code>UNBOUNDED PRECEDING</code>: Select from the beginning of the column/partition</li>
<li><code>UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING</code>: Select to the end of the column/partition</li>
<li><code>CURRENT ROW</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Can be used to calculate running totals, sums, averages, etc</li>
<li>Can also be partitioned by one or more columns</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="4.3.1.-Example:-Sliding-Window-to-the-End">4.3.1. Example: Sliding Window to the End<a class="anchor-link" href="#4.3.1.-Example:-Sliding-Window-to-the-End">&#182;</a></h4><p>Sorting the data set in reverse order and calculating a backward running total from the CURRENT ROW to the end of the data set (earliest record).</p>

</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[80]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;SELECT </span>
<span class="s2">    -- Select the date, home goal, and away goals</span>
<span class="s2">    date,</span>
<span class="s2">    home_team_goal,</span>
<span class="s2">    away_team_goal,</span>
<span class="s2">    -- Create a running total and running average of home goals</span>
<span class="s2">    SUM(home_team_goal) OVER(ORDER BY date DESC</span>
<span class="s2">         ROWS BETWEEN CURRENT ROW AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING) AS running_total,</span>
<span class="s2">    AVG(home_team_goal) OVER(ORDER BY date DESC</span>
<span class="s2">         ROWS BETWEEN CURRENT ROW AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING) AS running_avg</span>
<span class="s2">FROM match</span>
<span class="s2">WHERE </span>
<span class="s2">    away_team_api_id = 9908 </span>
<span class="s2">    AND season = &#39;2011/2012&#39;;</span>
<span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
<span class="n">pd</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">read_sql</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">conn</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="output_wrapper">
<div class="output">


<div class="output_area">

    <div class="prompt output_prompt">Out[80]:</div>

<div class="cell border-box-sizing text_cell rendered"><div class="prompt input_prompt">
</div><div class="inner_cell">
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h3 id="4.4.-Case-Study:-Rivals-of-MU">4.4. Case Study: Rivals of MU<a class="anchor-link" href="#4.4.-Case-Study:-Rivals-of-MU">&#182;</a></h3><p><strong> Q: How badly did Manchester United (MU) lose in each match?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Setting up the home team CTE</li>
<li>Setting up the away team CTE</li>
<li>Join two CTEs together</li>
<li>Add a window function that rank the loses</li>
</ul>

</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[81]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;-- Set up the home team CTE</span>
<span class="s2">WITH home AS (</span>
<span class="s2">  SELECT m.id, t.team_long_name,</span>
<span class="s2">      CASE WHEN m.home_team_goal &gt; m.away_team_goal THEN &#39;MU Win&#39;</span>
<span class="s2">           WHEN m.home_team_goal &lt; m.away_team_goal THEN &#39;MU Loss&#39; </span>
<span class="s2">           ELSE &#39;Tie&#39; END AS outcome</span>
<span class="s2">  FROM match AS m</span>
<span class="s2">  LEFT JOIN team AS t ON m.home_team_api_id = t.team_api_id),</span>

<span class="s2">-- Set up the away team CTE</span>
<span class="s2">away AS (</span>
<span class="s2">  SELECT m.id, t.team_long_name,</span>
<span class="s2">      CASE WHEN m.home_team_goal &gt; m.away_team_goal THEN &#39;MU Loss&#39;</span>
<span class="s2">           WHEN m.home_team_goal &lt; m.away_team_goal THEN &#39;MU Win&#39; </span>
<span class="s2">           ELSE &#39;Tie&#39; END AS outcome</span>
<span class="s2">  FROM match AS m</span>
<span class="s2">  LEFT JOIN team AS t ON m.away_team_api_id = t.team_api_id)</span>

<span class="s2">-- Select columns and and rank the matches by date</span>
<span class="s2">SELECT DISTINCT</span>
<span class="s2">    date,</span>
<span class="s2">    home.team_long_name AS home_team,</span>
<span class="s2">    away.team_long_name AS away_team,</span>
<span class="s2">    m.home_team_goal, m.away_team_goal,</span>
<span class="s2">    RANK() OVER(ORDER BY ABS(home_team_goal - away_team_goal) DESC) as match_rank</span>

<span class="s2">-- Join the CTEs onto the match table</span>
<span class="s2">FROM match AS m</span>
<span class="s2">LEFT JOIN home ON m.id = home.id</span>
<span class="s2">LEFT JOIN away ON m.id = away.id</span>
<span class="s2">WHERE m.season = &#39;2014/2015&#39;</span>
<span class="s2">      AND ((home.team_long_name = &#39;Manchester United&#39; AND home.outcome = &#39;MU Loss&#39;)</span>
<span class="s2">      OR (away.team_long_name = &#39;Manchester United&#39; AND away.outcome = &#39;MU Loss&#39;));</span>
<span class="s2">&quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
<span class="n">pd</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">read_sql</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sql_stmt</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">conn</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">head</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="output_wrapper">
<div class="output">


<div class="output_area">

    <div class="prompt output_prompt">Out[81]:</div>
